class="_3bcz">alt</span>+<span class="_3bcz">/</span> 即可打开菜单</div></div></div></div></div><div id="globalContainer" class="uiContextualLayerParent"><div class="fb_content clearfix " id="content" role="main"><div class="_r6n _3m9" id="content"><div class="clearfix _r6o" id="cs-header"><div class="_r6p"><a href="/communitystandards/?fb_home" title="&#x9996;&#x9875;" class="_r6q"><i class="img sp_Mjwuy2IrTyK sx_71004d"></i></a><a class="_r6s" href="/communitystandards/"><span>社群守则</span></a></div></div><div class="_w_k"><div class="_4-u2 _w_j _4-u8"><div class="_w_l"></div><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7"><div class="_4bl9"> Facebook 的使命是赋予人们分享的力量，让世界变得更开放，让人们联系更紧密。人们每天可以通过 Facebook 分享自己的故事、通过他人的视野领略世界，以及与好友保持联系等。Facebook 上发生的对话体现了数十亿用户沟通的多样性。 <br /><br /> 我们希望用户能够安全自由地使用 Facebook，因此制定了以下社区守则。这些守则有助于您了解 Facebook 允许分享的内容，以及可能被举报和移除的内容。请记住，由于全球社区的多样性，您不赞同或对您造成干扰的某些内容可能并未违反 Facebook 社区守则。 </div><div class="_4bl7 _w_p"><a href="/communitystandards/video/" rel="dialog" role="button"></a><i class="_w_o img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_87ec5f"></i><a role="button" class="_42ft _4jy0 _55pi _2agf _4o_4 _w_n _4jy3 _4jy2 selected _51sy" href="/communitystandards/?letter" style="max-width:160px;" aria-haspopup="true"><span class="_55pe">查看 Facebook 团队来信</span></a></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_w_k"><div class="_4-u2 _w_j _4-u8" id="helping-to-keep-you-safe"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7 _2auw" id="helping-to-keep-you-safe"><div class="_4bl9">为保护你的安全而贡献力量</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">返回顶端<i class="_2auy img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_e48816"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_c44607"></i></div><div class="_4bl9"><div id="u_0_9"><span class="img _55ym _55yq _55yo _3kks" aria-busy="true" role="progressbar" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="100" aria-valuetext="&#x52a0;&#x8f7d;&#x4e2d;..."></span></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_w_k"><div class="_4-u2 _w_j _4-u8" id="encouraging-respectful-behavior"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7 _2auw" id="encouraging-respectful-behavior"><div class="_4bl9">鼓励礼貌行为</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">返回顶端<i class="_2auy img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_e48816"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_e03a5e"></i></div><div class="_4bl9"><div id="u_0_a"><span class="img _55ym _55yq _55yo _3kks" aria-busy="true" role="progressbar" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="100" aria-valuetext="&#x52a0;&#x8f7d;&#x4e2d;..."></span></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_w_k"><div class="_4-u2 _w_j _4-u8" id="keeping-your-account-secure"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7 _2auw" id="keeping-your-account-secure"><div class="_4bl9">保护帐户和个人信息安全</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">返回顶端<i class="_2auy img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_e48816"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_384b17"></i></div><div class="_4bl9"><div id="u_0_b"><span class="img _55ym _55yq _55yo _3kks" aria-busy="true" role="progressbar" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="100" aria-valuetext="&#x52a0;&#x8f7d;&#x4e2d;..."></span></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_w_k"><div class="_4-u2 _w_j _4-u8" id="protecting-your-intellectual-property"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7 _2auw" id="protecting-your-intellectual-property"><div class="_4bl9">保护个人知识产权</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">返回顶端<i class="_2auy img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_e48816"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_d6092c"></i></div><div class="_4bl9"><div id="u_0_c"><span class="img _55ym _55yq _55yo _3kks" aria-busy="true" role="progressbar" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="100" aria-valuetext="&#x52a0;&#x8f7d;&#x4e2d;..."></span></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_w_q"><div class="_w_j"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_2auw _3ma">举报违规内容</div><div class="_5aj7"><div class="_4bl9 _w_r"> Facebook 全球社区的用户数量与日俱增，我们致力于为大家打造一个不存在违规内容的社交环境。为此，我们需要包括您在内的所有用户共同努力。如果您认为某些内容违反 Facebook 条款，<a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/www/181495968648557">请向我们举报</a>。我们在全球有专门团队负责审核举报内容，确保 Facebook 的安全性。 <br /><br /> 政府有时也会要求我们删除违反当地法律但未违反 Facebook 社区守则的内容。如果在仔细分析法律依据之后，我们发现该内容违反了本地法律，那么会仅在相关国家或领土境内禁止访问该内容。 <br /><br /> 请记住以下几点： <br /><br /><ul class="_p7q"><li> 发现违反 Facebook 社区守则的内容后，我们就会采取以下行动。 </li><li> 我们可能要求主页所有者将自己的姓名和个人主页与包含残忍和麻木不仁内容的公共主页关联，不管这些内容是否违反 Facebook 政策。 </li><li> 被举报的内容不一定会被删除，因为这些内容可能并未违反 Facebook 政策。 </li><li> 我们的内容审核人员可能与您联系并询问某个帖子为什么违反了 Facebook 政策。举报内容时，请说明为什么应该删除该内容（例如，包含裸照或仇恨言论），以便我们将此转交给相关人员审核。 </li><li> 在获得有关特定帖子的额外信息或者发现某公共主页或个人主页上出现新的违规内容之后，我们可能会改变审核决定。 </li><li> 被举报的次数不作为删除相关内容的依据。Facebook 并不会只因为某内容被多次举报就将之删除。 </li><li> 违反社区守则的后果取决于违规的严重程度以及相应用户的 Facebook 历史记录。例如，对于首次违规，我们可能会先予警告；如果之后发现该用户继续违规，我们可能会限制其在 Facebook 发帖或者禁止其访问 Facebook。</li></ul><br /> 并非所有您不赞同或对您造成困扰的内容都违反了 Facebook 社区守则。因此，我们针对您看到的内容提供自定义与控制功能，如取消关注、拉黑和隐藏不想看到的帖子、用户、主页和应用，同时，我们鼓励您利用这些功能来提升自己的个性化体验。<a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/212722115425932">详细了解</a>。通常，用户还可以直接与某内容的发布者联系，解决相关问题。我们创建了各种<a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/www/128548343894719">工具</a>，以供用户与令其不快的帖子、照片或其他内容的发布者直接取得联系。 </div><div class="_4bl7 _w_p"><a role="button" class="_42ft _4jy0 _55pi _2agf _4o_4 _w_n _4jy3 _4jy2 selected _51sy" href="/help/181495968648557?ref=community_standards" style="max-width:160px;" aria-haspopup="true"><span class="_55pe">举报违规内容</span></a><a role="button" class="_42ft _4jy0 _55pi _2agf _4o_4 _w_n _4jy3 _517h _51sy" href="/help/212722115425932?ref=community_standards" style="max-width:160px;" aria-haspopup="true"><span class="_55pe">控制看到的内容</span></a><a role="button" class="_42ft href="/communitystandards/?fb_home" title="Home" class="_r6q"><i class="img sp_Mjwuy2IrTyK sx_71004d"></i></a><a class="_r6s" href="/communitystandards/"><span>Community Standards</span></a></div></div><div class="_w_k"><div class="_4-u2 _w_j _4-u8"><div class="_w_l"></div><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7"><div class="_4bl9"> Our mission is to give people the power to build community and bring the world closer together. Every day, people come to Facebook to share their stories, see the world through the eyes of others and connect with friends and causes. The conversations that happen on Facebook reflect the diversity of a community of more than two billion people. <br /><br /> We want people to feel safe when using Facebook. For that reason, we&#039;ve developed a set of Community Standards, outlined below. These policies will help you understand what type of sharing is allowed on Facebook, and what type of content may be reported to us and removed. Sometimes we will allow content if newsworthy, significant or important to the public interest – even if it might otherwise violate our standards. Because of the diversity of our global community, please keep in mind that something that may be disagreeable or disturbing to you may not violate our Community Standards. </div><div class="_4bl7 class="_w_j"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_2auw _3ma">Reporting Abuse</div><div class="_5aj7"><div class="_4bl9 _w_r"> Our global community is growing every day and we strive to welcome people to an environment free from abusive content. To do this, we rely on people like you. If you see something on Facebook that you believe violates our terms, <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/www/181495968648557">please report it to us</a>. We have dedicated teams working around the world to review things you report to help make sure Facebook remains safe. <br /><br /> Governments also sometimes ask us to remove content that violates local laws, but does not violate our Community Standards. If after careful legal review, we find that the content is illegal under local law, then we may make it unavailable only in the relevant country or territory. <br /><br /> Please keep the following in mind: <br /><br /><ul class="_p7q"><li> We may take action any time something violates the Community Standards outlined here. </li><li> We may ask Page owners to associate their name and Facebook Profile with a Page that contains cruel and insensitive content, even if that content does not violate our policies. </li><li> Reporting something doesn&#039;t guarantee that it will be removed because it may not violate our policies. </li><li> Our content reviewers will look to you for information about why a post may violate our policies. If you report content, please tell us why the content should be removed (e.g., is it nudity or hate speech?) so that we can send it to the right person for review. </li><li> Our review decisions may occasionally change after receiving additional context about specific posts or after seeing new, violating content appearing on a Page or Facebook Profile. </li><li> The number of reports does not impact whether something will be removed. We never remove content simply because it has been reported a number of times. </li><li> The consequences for violating our Community Standards vary depending on the severity of the violation and the person&#039;s history on Facebook. For instance, we may warn someone for a first violation, but if we continue to see further violations we may restrict a person&#039;s ability to post on Facebook or ban the person from Facebook.</li></ul><br /> Not all disagreeable or disturbing content violates our Community Standards. For this reason, we offer you the ability to customize and control what you see by unfollowing, blocking, and hiding the posts, people, Pages, and applications you don’t want to see – and we encourage you to use these controls to better personalize your experience. <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/212722115425932">Learn more</a>. People also often resolve issues they have about a piece of content by simply reaching out to the person who posted it. We’ve created <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/www/128548343894719">tools</a> for you to communicate directly with other people when you’re unhappy with posts, photos, or other content you see on Facebook. </div><div class="_4bl7 _w_p"><a role="button" class="_42ft _4jy0 _55pi _2agf _4o_4 _w_n _4jy3 _4jy2 selected _51sy" href="/help/181495968648557?ref=community_standards" We restrict the display of nudity and sexual activity because some audiences within our global community may be sensitive to this type of content - particularly because of their cultural background or age. In order to treat people fairly and respond to reports quickly, it is essential that we have policies in place that our global teams can apply uniformly and easily when reviewing content. As a result, our policies can sometimes be more blunt than we would like and restrict content shared for legitimate purposes. We are always working to get better at evaluating this content and enforcing our standards. \u003Cbr \/>\u003Cbr \/> We remove photographs of people displaying genitals or focusing in on fully exposed buttocks. We also restrict some images of female breasts if they include the nipple, but our intent is to allow images that are shared for medical or health purposes. We also allow photos of women actively engaged in breastfeeding or showing breasts with post-mastectomy scarring. We also allow photographs of paintings, sculptures, and other art that depicts nude figures.
